# Adventures_work_Data_Engineer_Project


## Project Overview
This project demonstrates an end-to-end data engineering solution using Azure services. The workflow includes extracting data from GitHub, ingesting it into Azure Data Lake, transforming it with Databricks, storing the transformed data back in the data lake, and creating a data warehouse in Synapse Analytics. Finally, the processed data is visualized using Power BI.

---

## Architecture
The solution is designed using the **Medallion Architecture**:
- **Bronze Layer**: Raw data from GitHub is ingested into Azure Data Lake.
- **Silver Layer**: Transformed and clean data is stored back in the data lake.
- **Gold Layer**: Aggregated and curated data is loaded into Synapse Analytics for analytical purposes.

---

## Tools and Technologies
- **Azure Data Factory (ADF)**: Orchestrates the data pipelines.
- **Azure Data Lake**: Stores raw and transformed data.
- **Azure Databricks**: Transforms the data using notebooks.
- **Azure Synapse Analytics**: Provides data warehousing capabilities.
- **Power BI**: Visualizes the data for business insights.
- **Git**: Source of raw data for ingestion.
- **Microsoft Entra ID**: Authentication and identity management.

---

## Solution Workflow
1. **Data Ingestion**:
   - Data is sourced from GitHub using Azure Data Factory (ADF).
   - ADF pipelines dynamically fetch data and load it into the Bronze layer of the data lake.

2. **Data Transformation**:
   - Azure Databricks processes and transforms the raw data using notebooks.
   - The clean, structured data is stored in the Silver layer of the data lake.

3. **Data Warehousing**:
   - Transformed data is ingested into Synapse Analytics for advanced analytics and reporting.

4. **Data Visualization**:
   - Power BI connects to Synapse Analytics to create interactive dashboards and reports.

---

## Key Features
### **Pipelines**
- Created a dynamic pipeline in ADF using:
  - **Lookup Activity**: Reads metadata for processing.
  - **ForEach Activity**: Iterates over datasets for dynamic processing.
  - **Copy Data Activity**: Transfers data between GitHub and the data lake.

### **Linked Services**
- Configured two linked services in ADF:
  1. **GitHub**: Connects to the data source.
  2. **Azure Data Lake**: Facilitates data storage.

---

## How to Run the Project
1. **Set Up Linked Services**:
   - Configure GitHub and Azure Data Lake linked services in Azure Data Factory.

2. **Run the ADF Pipeline**:
   - Use the dynamic pipeline to fetch data from GitHub and load it into the data lake.

3. **Execute Databricks Notebooks**:
   - Run transformation notebooks in Databricks to clean and process the data.

4. **Load Data into Synapse Analytics**:
   - Use Azure Synapse pipelines or scripts to load transformed data from the data lake.

5. **Visualize Data in Power BI**:
   - Connect Power BI to Synapse Analytics and create dashboards.

---

## Results
The project delivers an efficient and scalable data engineering solution, enabling:
- End-to-end data processing from ingestion to visualization.
- Dynamic and reusable pipelines in ADF.
- Clean and structured data storage using the Medallion Architecture.
- Advanced analytics with Synapse Analytics and actionable insights via Power BI.

---
